### ì§„ìˆ˜ë³€í™˜

```
a="212-44-58"; until [ "x$a" != "x" ]; do b=$(echo "obase=16; $(echo $a | awk -F- '{print $1}')" | bc); c=$(echo "obase=16; $(echo $a | awk -F- '{print $2}')" | bc); d=$(echo "obase=16; $(echo $a | awk -F- '{print $3}')" | bc); echo "$a => $b.$c.$d"; echo "----> Decimal Number like '$a':"; read a; done
212-44-58 => D42C3A
```

```
a="d42c3a"; until [ "x$a" != "x" ]; do printf "$a -> $((16#${a:0:2}))-$((16#${a:2:2}))-$((16#${a:4:2}))"; echo ""; echo "----> Hexa Number like '$a':"; read a; done
d42c3a -> 212-44-58
```

```
echo "obase=16 ; 113" | bc
#----> 10ì§„ìˆ˜'113'ì„ 16ì§„ìˆ˜ë¡œ ----> 71
echo $((0x71))
#----> 16ì§„ìˆ˜'71'ì„ 10ì§„ìˆ˜ë¡œ ----> 113

a=143 ; echo "obase=16;$a" | bc
#----> 8F
a=8f ; echo $((0x$a))
#----> 143
```


## Docker Compose ì„¤ì¹˜

ì¶œì²˜: Ubuntu Docker Compose ì„¤ì¹˜ ë°©ë²•(22.04 ê¸°ì¤€) 2023-02-15 by ë‚˜ë£¨ https://osg.kr/archives/2108

### 1ë‹¨ê³„: ì‹œìŠ¤í…œì— Docker ì €ì¥ì†Œ ì¶”ê°€

```
#-- HTTPS ê¸°ë°˜ ë¦¬í¬ì§€í† ë¦¬ë¥¼ ì‚¬ìš© í•˜ë ¤ë©´ ë‹¤ìŒ ë„¤ ê°€ì§€ íŒ¨í‚¤ì§€ê°€ í•„ìš”í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤ .
#-- ca-certificates- SSL/TLS ì¸ì¦ì„œë¥¼ í™•ì¸í•˜ëŠ” íŒ¨í‚¤ì§€ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.
#-- curl- HTTPSë¥¼ í¬í•¨í•œ ì—¬ëŸ¬ í”„ë¡œí† ì½œì„ ì§€ì›í•˜ëŠ” ë„ë¦¬ ì‚¬ìš©ë˜ëŠ” ë°ì´í„° ì „ì†¡ ë„êµ¬ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.
#-- gnupg- PGP(Pretty Good Privacy) ì•”í˜¸í™” ë„êµ¬ ì œí’ˆêµ°ì˜ ì˜¤í”ˆ ì†ŒìŠ¤ êµ¬í˜„ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.
#-- lsb-release- LSB(Linux Standard Base) ë²„ì „ì„ ë³´ê³ í•˜ê¸° ìœ„í•œ ìœ í‹¸ë¦¬í‹°
sudo apt install ca-certificates curl gnupg lsb-release
#-- Dockerì˜ GPG í‚¤ìš© ë””ë ‰í„°ë¦¬ë¥¼ ë§Œë“­ë‹ˆë‹¤.
sudo mkdir /etc/apt/demokeyrings
#-- Dockerì˜ ì €ì¥ì†Œë¥¼ ì‹ ì„
sudo curl -fsSL https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu/gpg | sudo gpg --dearmor -o /etc/apt/demokeyrings/demodocker.gpg
#-- ì‹œìŠ¤í…œì— Docker ì €ì¥ì†Œë¥¼ ì¶”ê°€
echo \
  "deb [arch=$(dpkg --print-architecture) signed-by=/etc/apt/demokeyrings/demodocker.gpg] https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu \
  $(lsb_release -cs) stable" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/docker.list
```

### 2ë‹¨ê³„: Docker Compose ë° ê´€ë ¨ íŒ¨í‚¤ì§€ ì„¤ì¹˜

```
sudo apt update -y
sudo apt install docker-ce docker-ce-cli containerd.io docker-compose-plugin
sudo docker --version ; sudo docker compose version ; sudo ctr version
```

### 1. Wiki.js ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ì™€ Docker-compose.yml íŒŒì¼ ë§Œë“¤ê¸°

### 2. docker-compose.yml íŒŒì¼

```
version: "3"
services:

  db:
    #-- raspi: image: postgres:11-alpine
    image: postgres:14.1-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: wikidb #-- wiki ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„
      POSTGRES_USER: imwiki #-- wikijs ì‚¬ìš©ì ì´ë¦„
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: wikiam9ho #-- wikijsrocks ë¹„ë²ˆ
    logging:
      driver: "none"
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - /home/docker/pgsql:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    container_name:
      pgsql

  wiki:
    #-- raspi: image: requarks/wiki:2
    image: requarks/wiki:2.5
    depends_on:
      - db
    environment:
      DB_TYPE: postgres
      DB_HOST: db
      DB_PORT: 5432
      DB_NAME: wikidb #-- wiki ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„
      DB_USER: imwiki #-- wikijs ì‚¬ìš©ì ì´ë¦„
      DB_PASS: wikiam9ho #-- wikijsrocks ë¹„ë²ˆ
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "9900:3000"
    container_name:
      wikijs
```

5. rclone ë‚´ì—­ í™•ì¸ ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸.
```
 cat rclone-all-list.sh
#!/bin/sh

ymd=$(date +%y%m%d-%H%M%S)
if [ ! -d ${ymd} ]; then
        mkdir ${ymd}
fi
temp_file=qqq_temp-${ymd}
size_file=total_size-${ymd}

echo "for cn in edone jjdrb jjone kaos1mi kaos2mi kaos3mi kaos4mi kaosngc swlibgc tpn1mi tpn2mi tpn3mi y5dnmi y5ncmi yosjgc ysw10mi yswone ;do echo \"----> \${cn}: \$(rclone size \${cn}: | grep size)\" ; done" > ${ymd}/${size_file}

cnt=100
#-- old_cloud_name: for cn in jjedone kaos1mi kaos2mi kaos3mi kaos4mi kaosngc swlibgc tpn1mi tpn2mi tpn3mi y5dnmi y5ncmi yosjgc ysw10mi

for CLOUD_NAME in edone jjdrb jjone kaos1mi kaos2mi kaos3mi kaos4mi kaosngc swlibgc tpn1mi tpn2mi tpn3mi tpn4mi y5dnmi y5ncmi yosjgc ysw10mi yswone
do
        dattim=$(date +%y%m%d%a%H%M%S)
        cnt=$((cnt + 1))
        echo "#----> (${cnt:(-2)}) ${CLOUD_NAME}:"
        rclone lsl ${CLOUD_NAME}: > ${temp_file}
        # ìœ ë‹‰ìŠ¤ ì‰˜ì—ì„œ ìŠ¤í˜ì´ìŠ¤ ì˜ë¦¬ì§€ ì•Šê²Œ ìœ ì§€í•˜ê³  ì½ëŠ” ë°©ë²• ë©œë²ˆì´ˆì´ 2016. 10. 29. 10:22 https://pangate.com/904
        while IFS= read -r ONE_LINE
        do
                if [ -z "${ONE_LINE}" ]; then
                        qqq="null line skip"
                else
                        ###echo "#----> (1) ONE_LINE ===${ONE_LINE}==="
                        #----> (1) ONE_LINE ===     4492 2023-01-06 07:45:48.000000000 ë¬¸ì„œ/YES24eBook/6f6a52790c9c428abcaaf053fb576fb9/OEBPS/Styles/style.css===


                        REM_a_LINE="rem ${ONE_LINE}" #-- ONE_LINE ì²˜ìŒì˜ ê³µë°±ì„ ì—†ì• ì§€ ì•Šê¸° ìœ„í•´ì„œ,
                        ###echo "#----> (2) REM_a_LINE ===${REM_a_LINE}==="
                        #----> (2) REM_a_LINE ===rem     4492 2023-01-06 07:45:48.000000000 ë¬¸ì„œ/YES24eBook/6f6a52790c9c428abcaaf053fb576fb9/OEBPS/Styles/style.css===

                        # rem     8597 2023-08-30 10:08:19.000000000 zalba/keepass-yswone.kdbx
                        # rem     1314 2023-08-03 14:07:58.000000000 ë°”íƒ• í™”ë©´/WinSCP.lnk
                        # rem       20 2023-01-05 16:26:38.000000000 ë¬¸ì„œ/YES24eBook/6f6a52790c9c428abcaaf053fb576fb9/mimetype
                        # rem 25721740 2023-04-21 13:10:12.000000000 ë¬¸ì„œ/YES24eBook/2b9292f57c52462a8103735ba629a845/2b9292f57c52462a8103735ba629a845.PDF
                        #arg1 arg2---- arg3_date- arg4_time--------- arg5---- ---- ---- ----

                        arg4_time=$(echo "${REM_a_LINE}" | awk -F" " '{print $4}')
                        ###echo "#----> (3) arg4_time ===${arg4_time}==="
                        #----> (3) arg4_time ===07:45:48.000000000===

                        rem_size_date=$(echo "${REM_a_LINE}" | awk -F"${arg4_time}" '{print $1}')
                        ###echo "#----> (4) rem_size_date ===${rem_size_date}==="
                        #----> (4) rem_size_date ===rem     4492 2023-01-06 ===

                        namoji=$(echo "${REM_a_LINE}" | awk -F"${arg4_time}" '{print $2}')
                        ###echo "#----> (5) namoji ===${namoji}==="
                        #----> (5) namoji === ë¬¸ì„œ/YES24eBook/6f6a52790c9c428abcaaf053fb576fb9/OEBPS/Styles/style.css===

                        ###echo "#----> (6) ===${rem_size_date}${arg4_time} ${CLOUD_NAME}:${namoji:1}==="
                        #----> (6) ===rem     4492 2023-01-06 07:45:48.000000000 yswone:ë¬¸ì„œ/YES24eBook/6f6a52790c9c428abcaaf053fb576fb9/OEBPS/Styles/style.css===

                        echo "${rem_size_date:3}${arg4_time} ${CLOUD_NAME}:${namoji:1}" >> ${ymd}/${cnt:(-2)}-${CLOUD_NAME}-${dattim}.lsl
                        #-- :3 ìœ¼ë¡œ 'rem' ì„ ë–¼ì–´ë‚´ê³ , namoji ì˜ ì•ì— ë¶™ì€ ' ' ê³µë°±ë„ :1 ë¡œ ë—¸ë‹¤.
                fi
        done < ${temp_file}
        echo "#----> (${cnt:(-2)}) ${CLOUD_NAME}: $(rclone size ${CLOUD_NAME}: | grep size)" >> ${ymd}/${size_file}
        tail -1 ${ymd}/${size_file}
done
rm -f ${temp_file}
echo "#----> (9) 7za a -mx=9 list-rclone-${ymd}.7z ${ymd} ; ls -l . ${ymd}"
#----> (9) 7za a -mx=9 lsl-rclone-230831-142555.7z 230831-142555 ; ls -l . 230831-142555
7za a -mx=9 lsl-rclone-${ymd}.7z ${ymd} ; ls -l . ${ymd}
```

6. rclone ì„¤ì¹˜í›„, ìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ì§€ë¥¼ ë“±ë¡í•˜ê¸° ì „ì— ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ì˜ ë²ˆí™”ë¥¼ ë³´ê¸° ìœ„í•´ì„œ ë‹¤ìŒ ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ë¡œ ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ ë‚´ì—­ì„ ë³´ê´€í–ˆë‹¤.
```
11:47:43í™”231114 yosj@ubuntusvr ~/bin
bin $ cat root-ls.sh
#!/bin/sh

#-- for cn in bin dev home lib32 libx32 media opt root sbin srv sys usr boot etc lib lib64 mnt proc run snap swap.img tmp var

for cn in $(ls /)
do
        ls_name=ls-alR.${cn}-$(date +%y%m%d%a-%H%M)
        echo "#-- sudo du -sh /${cn} > ${ls_name}"
        sudo du -sh /${cn} > ${ls_name}
        echo "#-- sudo ls -alR /${cn} >> ${ls_name}"
        sudo ls -alR /${cn} >> ${ls_name}
done
11:47:53í™”231114 yosj@ubuntusvr ~/bin
```

## mp4 to mp3

### Step 1: Install FFmpeg 


1. https://online-audio-converter.com/ko/ mp4 to mp3
2. Linuxì—ì„œ mp4 / mkv / WebM ë¯¸ë””ì–´ íŒŒì¼ì„ mp3ë¡œ ë³€í™˜í•˜ëŠ” ë° ì‚¬ìš©í•  ìˆ˜ìˆëŠ” ê°„ë‹¨í•œ bash ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ https://computingforgeeks.com/how-to-convert-mp4-to-mp3-on-linux/
- For Ubuntu / Debian:
```
for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done
sudo apt -y install ffmpeg lame
echo "ğŸ”” mp4-mp3 (1-1) ---------- sudo apt -y install ffmpeg lame"
```

- For Fedora:
```
for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done
sudo dnf -y install https://download1.rpmfusion.org/free/fedora/rpmfusion-free-release-$(rpm -E %fedora).noarch.rpm
sudo dnf -y install https://download1.rpmfusion.org/nonfree/fedora/rpmfusion-nonfree-release-$(rpm -E %fedora).noarch.rpm
sudo dnf -y install ffmpeg ffmpeg-devel lame
echo "ğŸ”” mp4-mp3 (1-2) ---------- sudo dnf -y install ..."
```

### Step 2: Download Conversion script

```
for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done
wget https://raw.githubusercontent.com/jmutai/dotfiles/master/scripts/mp3con.sh
echo "ğŸ”” mp4-mp3 (2-1) ---------- wget https://raw.githubusercontent.com/jmutai/dotfiles/master/scripts/mp3con.sh"
```
You can as well copy below script snippet.
```
#!/usr/bin/env bash

# My bash Script to convert mp4 to mp3
# By Josphat Mutai
# web: www.computingforgeeks.com
# email: kiplangatmtai@gmail.com

# Requires
# ffmpeg installed
# lame installed
# Check https://computingforgeeks.com/how-to-convert-mp4-to-mp3-on-linux/

echo -ne """
1: Current directory í˜„ì¬ì˜ ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ì—ì„œ ì²˜ë¦¬
2: Provide directory ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ë¥¼ ì§€ì •í•¨
"""
echo ""
echo -n "Selection : "
read selection

case $selection in
    1)
	echo "Okay.."
	echo ""
	echo "Current dir is `pwd` "
	;;
    2)
    echo ""
    echo -n "Give diretory name: "
    read dir_name

# Check if given directory is valid
if [ -d $dir_name ]; then
    
    cd "${$dir_name}"
    echo "Current directory is `pwd` "
    echo 
else
    echo "Invalid directory, exiting.."
    echo ""
    exit 10
fi

    echo
    ;;
    
   *)
       echo
       echo "Wrong selection"
       exit 11
       ;;
esac

echo ""

# Create dir to store mp3 files if it doesn't exist
# First get the current directory name

current_dir=`pwd`
base_name=` basename "$current_dir"`

if [[ ! -d "$base_name"-mp3 ]]; then
    
echo "$base_name" | xargs  -d "\n" -I {} mkdir {}-mp3
    echo ""
fi
echo ""


# Bigin to covert videos to mp3 audio files
# -d "\n" > Change delimiter from any whitespace to end of line character 

find . -name "*.mp4" -o -name "*.mkv" -o -name "*.webm" | xargs  -d "\n"  -I {} ffmpeg -i {} -b:a 320K -vn "$base_name"-mp3/{}.mp3 

# remove video extensions

cd "${base_name}"-mp3

for file_name in *; do      
    mv "$file_name" "`echo $file_name | sed  "s/.mp4//g;s/.mkv//g;s/.webm//g"`";
done

# Move audio directory to ~/ìŒì•…

if [[ ! -d ~/ìŒì•… ]]; then
    mkdir ~/ìŒì•…
fi
cd ..

mv  "$base_name"-mp3 ~/ìŒì•…/

# Check if conversion successfull

echo ""

if [[ $? -eq "0" ]];then
    echo " All files converted successfully"
else
    echo "Conversation failed"
    exit 1
fi
```

Make the script executable:
```
for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done
chmod +x mp3con.sh
echo "ğŸ”” mp4-mp3 (2-2) ---------- chmod +x mp3con.sh"
```

### Step 3: Convert mp4/mkv/WebM media files to mp3

```
for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done
sh mp3con.sh
echo "ğŸ”” mp4-mp3 (3-1) ---------- sh mp3con.sh"
```


## Brave in Debian, Ubuntu, Mint

```
sudo apt install curl

sudo curl -fsSLo /usr/share/keyrings/brave-browser-archive-keyring.gpg https://brave-browser-apt-release.s3.brave.com/brave-browser-archive-keyring.gpg

echo "deb [signed-by=/usr/share/keyrings/brave-browser-archive-keyring.gpg] https://brave-browser-apt-release.s3.brave.com/ stable main"|sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/brave-browser-release.list

sudo apt update

sudo apt install brave-browser
```

```

#-- ì˜ˆë¥¼ë“¤ì–´, ë¡œì»¬ ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ ì´ë¦„ì´ 'last-edit-231102' ë¼ë©´, ë‹¤ìŒê³¼ ê°™ì´ í•˜ë©´ ëœë‹¤.
onedrive --synchronize --single-directory 'last-edit-231102'
```

OneDrive ì—ì„œ í˜„ì¬ ë¡œì»¬ ìœ„ì¹˜ë¡œ ë‹¤ìš´ë¡œë“œë§Œ í•˜ë ¤ë©´,
```

```

ë¡œì»¬ì—ì„œ OneDrive ë¡œ ì—…ë¡œë“œë§Œ í•˜ë ¤ë©´,
```
onedrive --synchronize --upload-only
```

ìœ„ ì‘ì—…ì—ì„œ ë¡œì»¬ì—ëŠ” ì—†ëŠ” íŒŒì¼ì´ë‚˜ í´ë”ê°€ OneDrive ìª½ì— ìˆìœ¼ë©´, OneDrive ìª½ì—ë§Œ ìˆë˜ íŒŒì¼ì´ë‚˜ í´ë”ëŠ” ì‚­ì œí•˜ê²Œ ë˜ë¯€ë¡œ,
ë¡œì»¬ì—ëŠ” ì—†ì§€ë§Œ OneDrive ì—ëŠ” ìˆëŠ” ë°ì´í„°ëŠ” ê·¸ëƒ¥ ë³´ê´€í•´ì•¼ í•œë‹¤ë©´,
ë‹¤ìŒê³¼ ê°™ì´ ì›ê²©ì—ë§Œ ìˆëŠ” íŒŒì¼ì€ ì‚­ì œí•˜ì§€ ì•Šë„ë¡ ì§€ì •í•´ì¤˜ì•¼ í•œë‹¤.

2.á„€: Hangul jamo with a green background are modern-usage characters which can be converted into precomposed Hangul syllables under Unicode normalization form NFC.
Hangul jamo with a white background are used for archaic Korean only, and there are no corresponding precomposed Hangul syllables.
"Conjoining Jamo Behavior" (PDF). The Unicode Standard. March 2020.

## nodejs ë¥¼ ubuntu ì— ì„¤ì¹˜í•˜ê¸°

NodeSource Node.js Binary Distributions https://github.com/nodesource/distributions

1. Nodesource GPG í‚¤ ë‹¤ìš´ë¡œë“œ ë° ê°€ì ¸ ì˜¤ê¸°
```
for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done
sudo apt-get update
sudo apt-get install -y ca-certificates curl gnupg
sudo mkdir -p /etc/apt/keyrings
curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/gpgkey/nodesource-repo.gpg.key | sudo gpg --dearmor -o /etc/apt/keyrings/nodesource.gpg
echo "ğŸµ (1) --------"
```
2. deb ì €ì¥ì†Œ ë§Œë“¤ê¸°
```
for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done
NODE_MAJOR=21 # í•„ìš”í•œ ë²„ì „ 16,18,20,21
echo "deb [signed-by=/etc/apt/keyrings/nodesource.gpg] https://deb.nodesource.com/node_$NODE_MAJOR.x nodistro main" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/nodesource.list
echo "ğŸµ (2) --------"
```
3. ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ë° ì„¤ì¹˜
```
for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done
sudo apt-get update
sudo apt-get install nodejs -y
```

# Prisma CRUD êµ¬í˜„ (feat Prisma Studio)

âš’ Backend/Node.js by Fomagran ğŸ’» 2022. 8. 2. https://fomaios.tistory.com/entry/Nodejs-Prisma-CRUD-%EA%B5%AC%ED%98%84%ED%95%B4-%EB%B3%B4%EA%B8%B0-feat-Prisma-Studio

## 1. Init Prisma


## 2. Set a environment

.env íŒŒì¼ì— db ì •ë³´ ì…ë ¥.
```
for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done
cat >> .env << __EOF__

DATABASE_URL="postgresql://imwiki:wikiam9ho@localhost:5432/wikidb?schema=public"
# DATABASE_URL="ë””ë¹„ì¢…ë¥˜://ìœ ì €ì´ë¦„:íŒ¨ìŠ¤ì›Œë“œ@localhost:í¬íŠ¸ë²ˆí˜¸/ë””ë¹„ì´ë¦„"
__EOF__
echo "(2-1) tail .env"

echo "ğŸµ (2-2) --------"
```

## 3. Set a schema.prisma

```

```

`cat prisma/schema.prisma` íŒŒì¼ ë‚´ìš©:
```
// This is your Prisma schema file,
// learn more about it in the docs: https://pris.ly/d/prisma-schema

generator client {
  provider = "prisma-client-js"
}

datasource db {
  provider = "postgresql"
  url      = env("DATABASE_URL") #-- .env ì— ì„ ì–¸í•œ ê²ƒì„ ì“´ë‹¤.
}
```

ê·¸ë¦¬ê³  ë‚˜ì„œ, Gagyebu ë¼ê³  ì´ë¦„ì„ ì§€ì€ í…Œì´ë¸”ì—, ì›í•˜ëŠ” ë°ì´í„° ëª¨ë¸ì„ ì •ì˜í•´ ì¤€ë‹¤.
```
for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done
tee Gagyebu_table_init << __EOF__
model Gagyebu {
  id        Int      @id @default(autoincrement())
  pum       String   @db.VarChar(255)
  su        Int      @default(0)
  dan       Int      @default(0)
  kum       Int      @default(0)
  gage      String   @db.VarChar(255)
  jibul     Int
  ymd       String
  hm        String
  bigo      String   @db.VarChar(255)
  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt
}
__EOF__
echo "(3-2) cat Gagyebu_table_init"
cat Gagyebu_table_init
echo "ğŸµ (3-3) --------"
```

```
a="212-44-58"; until [ "x$a" != "x" ]; do b=$(echo "obase=16; $(echo $a | awk -F- '{print $1}')" | bc); c=$(echo "obase=16; $(echo $a | awk -F- '{print $2}')" | bc); d=$(echo "obase=16; $(echo $a | awk -F- '{print $3}')" | bc); echo "$a => $b.$c.$d"; echo "----> Decimal Number like '$a':"; read a; done
212-44-58 => D42C3A
```

```
a="d42c3a"; until [ "x$a" != "x" ]; do printf "$a -> $((16#${a:0:2}))-$((16#${a:2:2}))-$((16#${a:4:2}))"; echo ""; echo "----> Hexa Number like '$a':"; read a; done
d42c3a -> 212-44-58
```

```
echo "obase=16 ; 113" | bc
#----> 10ì§„ìˆ˜'113'ì„ 16ì§„ìˆ˜ë¡œ ----> 71
echo $((0x71))
#----> 16ì§„ìˆ˜'71'ì„ 10ì§„ìˆ˜ë¡œ ----> 113

a=143 ; echo "obase=16;$a" | bc
#----> 8F
a=8f ; echo $((0x$a))
#----> 143
```


## Ubuntu Docker Compose ì„¤ì¹˜

ì¶œì²˜: Ubuntu Docker Compose ì„¤ì¹˜ ë°©ë²•(22.04 ê¸°ì¤€) 2023-02-15 by ë‚˜ë£¨ https://osg.kr/archives/2108

### 1ë‹¨ê³„: ì‹œìŠ¤í…œì— Docker ì €ì¥ì†Œ ì¶”ê°€

```
#-- HTTPS ê¸°ë°˜ ë¦¬í¬ì§€í† ë¦¬ë¥¼ ì‚¬ìš© í•˜ë ¤ë©´ ë‹¤ìŒ ë„¤ ê°€ì§€ íŒ¨í‚¤ì§€ê°€ í•„ìš”í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤ .
#-- ca-certificates- SSL/TLS ì¸ì¦ì„œë¥¼ í™•ì¸í•˜ëŠ” íŒ¨í‚¤ì§€ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.
#-- curl- HTTPSë¥¼ í¬í•¨í•œ ì—¬ëŸ¬ í”„ë¡œí† ì½œì„ ì§€ì›í•˜ëŠ” ë„ë¦¬ ì‚¬ìš©ë˜ëŠ” ë°ì´í„° ì „ì†¡ ë„êµ¬ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.
#-- gnupg- PGP(Pretty Good Privacy) ì•”í˜¸í™” ë„êµ¬ ì œí’ˆêµ°ì˜ ì˜¤í”ˆ ì†ŒìŠ¤ êµ¬í˜„ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.
#-- lsb-release- LSB(Linux Standard Base) ë²„ì „ì„ ë³´ê³ í•˜ê¸° ìœ„í•œ ìœ í‹¸ë¦¬í‹°
sudo apt install ca-certificates curl gnupg lsb-release
#-- Dockerì˜ GPG í‚¤ìš© ë””ë ‰í„°ë¦¬ë¥¼ ë§Œë“­ë‹ˆë‹¤.
sudo mkdir /etc/apt/demokeyrings
#-- Dockerì˜ ì €ì¥ì†Œë¥¼ ì‹ ì„
sudo curl -fsSL https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu/gpg | sudo gpg --dearmor -o /etc/apt/demokeyrings/demodocker.gpg
#-- ì‹œìŠ¤í…œì— Docker ì €ì¥ì†Œë¥¼ ì¶”ê°€
echo \
  "deb [arch=$(dpkg --print-architecture) signed-by=/etc/apt/demokeyrings/demodocker.gpg] https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu \
  $(lsb_release -cs) stable" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/docker.list
```

## Docker Compose ë¥¼ ì´ìš©í•œ Wiki.Js ì„¤ì¹˜í•˜ê¸°

ì¶œì²˜: ë‹¬ì†Œì”¨ì˜ í•˜ë£¨ https://blog.dalso.org/article/docker-compose%EB%A5%BC-%EC%9D%B4%EC%9A%A9%ED%95%9C-wiki-js-%EC%84%A4%EC%B9%98%ED%95%98%EA%B8%B0

### 2. docker-compose.yml íŒŒì¼

```
version: "3"
services:

  db:
    #-- raspi: image: postgres:11-alpine
    image: postgres:14.1-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: wikidb #-- wiki ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„
      POSTGRES_USER: imwiki #-- wikijs ì‚¬ìš©ì ì´ë¦„
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: wikiam9ho #-- wikijsrocks ë¹„ë²ˆ
    logging:
      driver: "none"
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - /home/docker/pgsql:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    container_name:
      pgsql

  wiki:
    #-- raspi: image: requarks/wiki:2
    image: requarks/wiki:2.5
    depends_on:
      - db
    environment:
      DB_TYPE: postgres
      DB_HOST: db
      DB_PORT: 5432
      DB_NAME: wikidb #-- wiki ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„
      DB_USER: imwiki #-- wikijs ì‚¬ìš©ì ì´ë¦„
      DB_PASS: wikiam9ho #-- wikijsrocks ë¹„ë²ˆ
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "9900:3000"
    container_name:
      wikijs
```

2. ë°±ì—…ë°›ì•˜ë˜ zzz `${zzz}` ì••ì¶•íŒŒì¼ì„ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ë¡œ ì—…ë¡œë“œ

```
      'y' ë¥¼ ëˆ„ë¥´ë©´, í˜„ì¬ì˜ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ê°€ ëª¨ë‘ ì§€ì›Œì§€ê³ ,
                    ì´ì „ì— ë°±ì—…ë°›ì•˜ë˜ ${zzz} ë‚´ìš©ìœ¼ë¡œ ì±„ì›Œì§‘ë‹ˆë‹¤.

    echo "----> sudo docker ps -a ; sudo ${ggg}docker stop${xxx} ${WIKI_CONTAINER} ; sudo docker ps -a"
    sudo docker ps -a ; sudo docker stop ${WIKI_CONTAINER} ; sudo docker ps -a

    time sudo docker exec -it ${DATABASE_CONTAINER} dropdb -U ${DB_user_NAME} ${DATABASE_NAME}

    time sudo docker exec -it ${DATABASE_CONTAINER} createdb -U ${DB_user_NAME} ${DATABASE_NAME}

    echo "----> ë¹„ë²ˆì„ ì…ë ¥í•˜ì„¸ìš”:"

    time 7za x -so ${zzz} | sudo docker exec -i ${DATABASE_CONTAINER} psql -U ${DB_user_NAME} ${DATABASE_NAME}
    echo "----> sudo docker ${ggg}start${xxx} ${WIKI_CONTAINER} ; sudo docker ps -a"
    sudo docker start ${WIKI_CONTAINER} ; sudo docker ps -a
else
    echo "[ $a ] = ì—…ë¡œë“œë¥¼ ì·¨ì†Œí•¨."
```

### 2ë‹¨ê³„: Docker Compose ë° ê´€ë ¨ íŒ¨í‚¤ì§€ ì„¤ì¹˜

```
sudo apt update -y
sudo apt install docker-ce docker-ce-cli containerd.io docker-compose-plugin
sudo docker --version ; sudo docker compose version ; sudo ctr version
```

### 3ë‹¨ê³„: YAML íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±

```
mkdir ~/composedemo ; cd ~/composedemo ; vi docker-compose.yml
```
```
# Define services for our configuration. Parameters are similar to those defined by Docker at https://docs.docker.com/samples/wordpress/
services:
  # Create the MariaDB service
  db:
    # Specify the image version to pull from Docker Hub
    image: mariadb:10.6.4-focal
    # Run the command below to configure MariaDB to use the mysql_native_password authentication method
    command: '--default-authentication-plugin=mysql_native_password'
    # Define a storage volume for the database
    volumes:
      - database_data:/var/lib/mysql
    # Always restart the container
    restart: always
    # Define environment variables for the MariaDB root password, database name, user, and user password
    environment:
      - MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD=yourstrongrootpassword
      - MYSQL_DATABASE=wordpress
      - MYSQL_USER=cherry
      - MYSQL_PASSWORD=pepperandegg
    # Define the ports to expose to other containers on the same Docker network
    # These ports are NOT exposed externally to the host
    expose:
      - 3306
      - 33060
  # Create the MariaDB service
  wordpress:
    # Use the latest WordPress image from Docker Hub
    image: wordpress:latest
    # Create a storage volume for the WordPress site
    volumes:
      - wordpress_data:/var/www/html
    # Map port 8081 on the host to port 80 on the container
    ports:
      - 8081:80
    # Always restart the container
    restart: always
    # Use environment variables to allow WordPress to communicate with the database service
    environment:
      - WORDPRESS_DB_HOST=db
      - WORDPRESS_DB_USER=cherry
      - WORDPRESS_DB_PASSWORD=pepperandegg
      - WORDPRESS_DB_NAME=wordpress
# Define the top level volumes
volumes:
    database_data:
    wordpress_data:
```

### 4ë‹¨ê³„: Docker Composeë¥¼ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì—¬ ì•± ì‹¤í–‰

```
sudo docker compose up -d
```

### 5ë‹¨ê³„: ì•± í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸

ì´ì œ ë‹¤ìŒ ëª…ë ¹ì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì—¬ WordPress ë° MySQL ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆê°€ ì‹¤í–‰ë˜ê³  ìˆëŠ”ì§€ í™•ì¸í•  ìˆ˜ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
```
sudo docker compose ps
```

### 6ë‹¨ê³„: Docker Composeë¡œ ì¼ì‹œ ì¤‘ì§€ ë° ì¤‘ì§€

ì¼ì‹œ ì¤‘ì§€
```
sudo docker compose pause
```

ì¼ì‹œì¤‘ì§€ í•´ì œ
```
sudo docker compose unpause
```

ì¤‘ì§€
```
sudo docker compose stop
```

ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆë¥¼ ì¤‘ì§€í•˜ê³  ì—°ê²°ëœ ë„¤íŠ¸ì›Œí¬ë¥¼ ì œê±°í•˜ë ¤ë©´ ë‹¤ìŒ ëª…ë ¹ì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
```

```

### 7ë‹¨ê³„: ë°ëª¨ êµ¬ì„± ì‚­ì œ

ë°ëª¨ ì•±ìœ¼ë¡œ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ë¥¼ ë§ˆì¹œ í›„ì—ëŠ” êµ¬ì„± íŒŒì¼ì„ ì‚­ì œí•  ìˆ˜ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

## [OrangePi zero] ì™€ì´íŒŒì´ ì„¤ì •í•˜ê¸°

https://blogbicha.tistory.com/13

```
cd /etc/network
ls
vi interfaces
--------
source /etc/network/interface.d/*
# Network is managed by Network manager
auto lo
iface lo inet loopback

auto eth0
allow-hotplug eth0
iface eth0 inet dhcp

allow hotplug wlan0
iface wlan0 inet manual
wpa-roam /etc/wpa_supplicant/wpa_supplicant.conf
iface default inet dhcp
--------
cd /etc/wpa_supplicant
vi wpa_supplicant.conf
--------
ctrl_interface=DIR=/var/run/wpa_supplicant GROUP=netdev
update_config=1

network={
ssud=" ì™€ì´íŒŒì´ ì´ë¦„ "
psk=" ì™€ì´íŒŒì´ ë¹„ë²ˆ "
}
--------
sudo reboot
```

```
#
# Each task to run has to be defined through a single line
# indicating with different fields when the task will be run
```

## 2. wiki.js ìš© ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì„œë¹„ìŠ¤

```
lll=$(tput bold)$(tput setaf 0); rrr=$(tput bold)$(tput setaf 1); ggg=$(tput bold)$(tput setaf 2); yyy=$(tput bold)$(tput setaf 3); bbb=$(tput bold)$(tput setaf 4); mmm=$(tput bold)$(tput setaf 5); ccc=$(tput bold)$(tput setaf 6); www=$(tput bold)$(tput setaf 7); xxx=$(tput bold)$(tput sgr0); uuu=$(tput cuu 2)

for i in {0..3}; do echo "#"; done

#----> wiki.js ë„ì»¤ì—ì„œ ì“°ëŠ” bash ë³€ìˆ˜ ì„ ì–¸.
#--
DOCKER_DIR="/home/docker" #----- dwjs ë„ì»¤ ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ í™ˆ

DATABASE_SERVICE="db_srv" #----- dwjs ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì„œë¹„ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„
DATABASE_NAME="wikidb" #-------- dwjs ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„
DATABASE_CONTAINER="pgwikic" #-- dwjs ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆ ì´ë¦„
DB_user_NAME="imwiki" #--------- dwjs ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìœ ì € ì´ë¦„
DB_user_PASS="wikipswd" #------- dwjs ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìœ ì € ë¹„ë²ˆ
WIKI_SERVICE="wiki_srv" #---- dwjs ìœ„í‚¤ ì„œë¹„ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„
if [ "x${WIKI_PORT_NO}" = "x" ]; then
    WIKI_PORT_NO="7700" #-------- dwjs ìœ„í‚¤ í¬íŠ¸ ë²ˆí˜¸
fi
WIKI_CONTAINER="wikijsc" #--- dwjs ìœ„í‚¤ ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆ
CLOUD_NAME="tpn3mi" #--------- dwjs rclone ë°±ì—…ìš© í´ë¼ìš°ë“œ ì´ë¦„
LOCAL_BACKUP_DIR="${DOCKER_DIR}/backup/${DATABASE_CONTAINER}" #-- dwjs ì••ì¶•í•œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ë°±ì—… ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬
#--
#<---- wiki.js ë„ì»¤ì—ì„œ ì“°ëŠ” bash ë³€ìˆ˜ ì„ ì–¸.

if [ -d ${DATABASE_DIR} ]; then
    echo "(2-1) sudo ls -alR ${DATABASE_DIR}"
    sudo ls -alR ${DATABASE_DIR}
    cat <<__EOF__
(2-2) ${DATABASE_DIR} ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ê°€ ìˆìœ¼ë¯€ë¡œ,
      ë‚´ìš©ì„ í™•ì¸í•´ë´ì„œ ì“°ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ” ê²ƒì´ë©´,
      ì´ ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ë¥¼ ì§€ìš°ê³  ë‹¤ì‹œ ë§Œë“¤ê¸° ìœ„í•´,
          í„°ë¯¸ë„ì„ ìƒˆë¡œ ì—´ê³ ,
          ë‹¤ìŒì˜ ëª…ë ¹ì„ ì…ë ¥í—ˆì„¸ìš”.

      sudo rm -rf ${DATABASE_DIR}

ğŸ–ï¸ (2-3) í„°ë¯¸ë„ì„ ìƒˆë¡œ ì—´ê³  ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ ì¬í™•ì¸ Enter:
__EOF__
    read a
else
    echo "(2-4) ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ê°€ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ëŠ” ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ ë§Œë“¤ê¸°: sudo mkdir -p ${DATABASE_DIR}"
    sudo mkdir -p ${DATABASE_DIR}
```

## 3. ìœ„í‚¤ ì„œë¹„ìŠ¤

```
DATABASE_CONTAINER="pgwikic" #-- dwjs ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆ ì´ë¦„
DB_user_NAME="imwiki" #--------- dwjs ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìœ ì € ì´ë¦„
DB_user_PASS="wikipswd" #------- dwjs ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìœ ì € ë¹„ë²ˆ
WIKI_SERVICE="wiki_srv" #---- dwjs ìœ„í‚¤ ì„œë¹„ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„
if [ "x${WIKI_PORT_NO}" = "x" ]; then
    WIKI_PORT_NO="7700" #-------- dwjs ìœ„í‚¤ í¬íŠ¸ ë²ˆí˜¸
fi
WIKI_CONTAINER="wikijsc" #--- dwjs ìœ„í‚¤ ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆ
CLOUD_NAME="tpn3mi" #--------- dwjs rclone ë°±ì—…ìš© í´ë¼ìš°ë“œ ì´ë¦„
LOCAL_BACKUP_DIR="${DOCKER_DIR}/backup/${DATABASE_CONTAINER}" #-- dwjs ì••ì¶•í•œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ë°±ì—… ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬
#--
#<---- wiki.js ë„ì»¤ì—ì„œ ì“°ëŠ” bash ë³€ìˆ˜ ì„ ì–¸.

if [ ! -d ${YML_DIR} ]; then
    echo "(3-1) docker-compose.yml ë³´ê´€ ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ ë§Œë“¤ê¸°: sudo mkdir -p ${YML_DIR} ; sudo chmod 755 ${YML_DIR} ; sudo chown ${USER}:${USER} ${YML_DIR}"
    sudo mkdir -p ${YML_DIR} ; sudo chmod 755 ${YML_DIR} ; sudo chown ${USER}:${USER} ${YML_DIR}
fi

echo "ğŸ–ï¸ (3-2) Wiki.js ì˜ í¬íŠ¸ ë²ˆí˜¸: [ ${WIKI_PORT_NO} ]"
read a
if [ "x$a" != "x" ]; then
    WIKI_PORT_NO=$a
fi

echo "(3-3) ${YML_NAME} íŒŒì¼ì„ ë§Œë“­ë‹ˆë‹¤: cat > ${YML_NAME} <<__EOF__"
cat > ${YML_NAME} <<__EOF__
version: "3"
services:
  ${DATABASE_SERVICE}:
    image: postgres:11-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: ${DB_user_NAME}
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_user_PASS}
      POSTGRES_DB: ${DATABASE_NAME}
    logging:
      driver: "none"
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - ${DATABASE_DIR}:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    container_name:
      ${DATABASE_CONTAINER}

  ${WIKI_SERVICE}:
    image: requarks/wiki:2
    depends_on:
      - ${DATABASE_SERVICE}
    environment:
      DB_TYPE: postgres
      DB_HOST: ${DATABASE_SERVICE}
      DB_PORT: 5432
      DB_USER: ${DB_user_NAME}
      DB_PASS: ${DB_user_PASS}
      DB_NAME: ${DATABASE_NAME}
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "${WIKI_PORT_NO}:3000"
    container_name:
      ${WIKI_CONTAINER}
__EOF__

echo "(3-4) ls -lR ${YML_NAME} ; cat ${YML_NAME}"
ls -lR ${YML_NAME} ; cat ${YML_NAME}

echo "ğŸ¶ (3-5) --------------------"
```

## 6. ë°±ì—…íŒŒì¼ì„ DB ì— ë„ë¡œë‹´ëŠ” ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ ì‘ì—…

1. êµ¬ê¸€ í´ë¼ìš°ë“œë¡œ ë°±ì—…í–ˆë˜ wiki.js db íŒŒì¼ì„ ë¡œì»¬ í´ë”ë¡œ ë³µì‚¬í•œë‹¤.

`ë°±ì—… backup`: í˜„ì¬ì˜ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ë¥¼ **wikipg-220907ìˆ˜-1802-proenpi4b.sql.7z** ì™€ ê°™ì€ ì´ë¦„ìœ¼ë¡œ ì••ì¶•í•´ì„œ ì €ì¥í•œë‹¤.
`ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ restore`: ì••ì¶•í•´ì„œ ë³´ê´€í–ˆë˜ ë°±ì—… íŒŒì¼ì„ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ì— ë„ë¡œ ë¶€ì–´ ë‹´ëŠ”ë‹¤.
`í˜„ì¬ ìƒíƒœì˜ ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ë°±ì—…`: ë°±ì—…íŒŒì¼ì„ ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ í•˜ëŠ” ê²½ìš°, í˜„ì¬ì˜ db ì— ë“¤ì–´ìˆë˜ ë°ì´í„°ëŠ” ë°±ì—…íŒŒì¼ì— ì˜í•´ ì§€ì›Œì§„ë‹¤. ê·¸ë˜ì„œ ì¼ë‹¨ í˜„ì¬ìƒíƒœì˜ db ë¥¼ **" last-\${DATABASE_CONTAINER}-\$(date +%y%m%d_%H%M%S)-\$(uname -n).sql.7z "** ë“±ìœ¼ë¡œ ë°±ì—…í•˜ê³ ì„œ ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ í•˜ê¸° ìœ„í•´ì„œ ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ë°±ì—…ì„ ì‹¤ì‹œí•œë‹¤.

```
WIKI_SERVICE="wiki_srv" #---- dwjs ìœ„í‚¤ ì„œë¹„ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„
if [ "x${WIKI_PORT_NO}" = "x" ]; then
    WIKI_PORT_NO="7700" #-------- dwjs ìœ„í‚¤ í¬íŠ¸ ë²ˆí˜¸
fi
WIKI_CONTAINER="wikijsc" #--- dwjs ìœ„í‚¤ ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆ
CLOUD_NAME="tpn3mi" #--------- dwjs rclone ë°±ì—…ìš© í´ë¼ìš°ë“œ ì´ë¦„
LOCAL_BACKUP_DIR="${DOCKER_DIR}/backup/${DATABASE_CONTAINER}" #-- dwjs ì••ì¶•í•œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ë°±ì—… ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬
#--
#<---- wiki.js ë„ì»¤ì—ì„œ ì“°ëŠ” bash ë³€ìˆ˜ ì„ ì–¸.

#--> ë¡œì»¬ê³¼ ì›ê²© ë³´ê´€ì¥ì†Œ
this_y4m2=$(date +%Y)-$(date +%m) #- 2022-08
LOCAL_Y2M2=${LOCAL_BACKUP_DIR}/${this_y4m2}
if [ ! -d ${LOCAL_Y2M2} ]; then
    echo "(6-1) ${LOCAL_Y2M2} ë¡œì»¬ ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ë¥¼ ë§Œë“­ë‹ˆë‹¤: mkdir -p ${LOCAL_Y2M2}"
    mkdir -p ${LOCAL_Y2M2}
fi

#<-- ë¡œì»¬ê³¼ ì›ê²© ë³´ê´€ì¥ì†Œ

#-- ----> ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ íŒŒì¼ì´ ìˆìœ¼ë©´ í˜„ì¬ì˜ DB ë¥¼ ë°±ì—…í•˜ê³  ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ í•œë‹¤.
if [ "x$zzz" = "x" ]; then
    zzz="$(ls -ltr ${LOCAL_BACKUP_DIR}}/*.7z | tail -1 | awk '{print $9}')"
fi
echo "(6-2) ls -lR ${LOCAL_BACKUP_DIR} #--- ë°±ì—… ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ ë‚´ìš©"
ls -lR ${LOCAL_BACKUP_DIR}
echo "ğŸ–ï¸ (6-3) ì „ì²´ ê²½ë¡œë¥¼ ë‹¤ ì§€ì •í•˜ëŠ” ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ íŒŒì¼ì„ ì…ë ¥í•˜ì„¸ìš”: [ ${zzz} ]"
read a
if [ "x$a" = "x" ]; then
    a=${zzz}
fi
zzz=${a}

if [ "x${zzz}" = "x" ] || [ ! -f "${zzz}" ]; then
    #-- ----> ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ íŒŒì¼ì´ ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ì—¬ê¸°ì„œ ëëƒ„.
    cat <<__EOF__
||| (6-2) ls -lR ${LOCAL_BACKUP_DIR} #--- ë°±ì—… ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ ë‚´ìš©
$(ls -lR ${LOCAL_BACKUP_DIR})
|||
||| (6-3) ì§€ì •í•œ (ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ í• ) ${zzz} íŒŒì¼ì´ ì¡´ì¬í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
|||
||| ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ í•  íŒŒì¼ ì´ë¦„ì´ "${LOCAL_Y2M2}" ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ì— ìˆëŠ”
||| "last-${DATABASE_CONTAINER}-\$(date +%y%m%d_%H%M%S)-$(uname -n).sql.7z" ì¸ ê²½ìš°:
|||
||| zzz="${LOCAL_Y2M2}/last-${DATABASE_CONTAINER}-\$(date +%y%m%d_%H%M%S)-$(uname -n).sql.7z"
|||
||| (ë³µêµ¬í•˜ë ¤ëŠ” íŒŒì¼ ì´ë¦„ì„ ë‹´ì€ í™˜ê²½ ë³€ìˆ˜ì˜ ì´ë¦„ì´ 'zzz' ì„.)
|||
||| ì´ì™€ ê°™ì´ Bash Terminal ì—ì„œ ì„ ì–¸í•˜ê³  ë‚˜ì„œ, ì´ ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ë¥¼ ë‹¤ì‹œ ì‹¤í–‰í•´ì•¼ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
|||
ğŸ¶ (6-4) ${zzz} íŒŒì¼ì´ ì—†ìœ¼ë¯€ë¡œ ì‘ì—…ì„ ì¤‘ë‹¨í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
__EOF__
    #-- <---- ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ íŒŒì¼ì´ ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ì—¬ê¸°ì„œ ëëƒ„.
else
    #-- ----> ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ í•  .7z íŒŒì¼ì´ ìˆë‹¤.
    sql_name=$(basename ${zzz}) # ë°±ì—…íŒŒì¼ ì´ë¦„ë§Œ êº¼ëƒ„
    sql_dir=${zzz%/$sql_name} # ë°±ì—…íŒŒì¼ ì´ë¦„ì„ ë¹¼ê³  ë‚˜ë¨¸ì§€ ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ë§Œ ë‹´ìŒ
    cat <<__EOF__

ğŸ–ï¸ (6-5) í˜„ì¬ì˜ DB ë¥¼ ë°±ì—…í•˜ì§€ ì•Šìœ¼ë ¤ë©´, ì†Œë¬¸ì 'n' ì„ ëˆŒëŸ¬ ì£¼ì„¸ìš”."
__EOF__
    read N_is_current_no_backup ; echo "${uuu}"
    if [ "x${N_is_current_no_backup}" != "xn" ]; then
        N_is_current_no_backup="y"
    fi
    echo "[ í˜„ì¬ DB ë¥¼ ë°±ì—… = ${N_is_current_no_backup} ]"

    echo "qq1----> N_is_current_no_backup = [ ${N_is_current_no_backup} ]"
    echo "qq1----> restore_only = [ ${restore_only} ]"

    #-- --> 'ë°±ì—… ë°›ê¸° ì „' ìœ„í‚¤ ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆ ì •ì§€
    cat <<__EOF__
(6-6) ë°±ì—…ì„ ì‹œì‘í•˜ê¸°ì „ ìœ„í‚¤ ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆë¥¼ ë©ˆì¶¥ë‹ˆë‹¤.
      sudo docker ps -a ; sudo docker stop ${WIKI_CONTAINER} ; sudo docker ps -a
__EOF__
    sudo docker ps -a ; sudo docker stop ${WIKI_CONTAINER} ; sudo docker ps -a
    #-- <-- 'ë°±ì—… ë°›ê¸° ì „' ìœ„í‚¤ ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆ ì •ì§€

    if [ "x$N_is_current_no_backup" = 'xn' ]; then
        #-- ----> í˜„ì¬ì˜ DB ë¥¼ ë°±ì—…í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ”ë‹¤ ì„ íƒ.
        cat <<__EOF__
# |
# |
# |
# |
# |
# | !!!! ì£¼ì˜ !!!! í˜„ì¬ DB ë¥¼ ë‹¤ìš´ë¡œë“œ + ë°±ì—…í•˜ì§€ ì•Šê³ , ì—…ë¡œë“œ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
# |
# | ì—¬ê¸°ì„œ ì†Œë¬¸ì 'y' ë¥¼ ëˆ„ë¥´ë©´ í˜„ì¬ì˜ DB ë°±ì—…ì„ í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
# |
# | ë‹¤ë¥¸ ê¸€ìê±°ë‚˜ ê·¸ëƒ¥ Enter ë¥¼ ëˆ„ë¥´ë©´ ë°±ì—…ì´ ì§„í–‰ë©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
# |
ğŸ–ï¸ (6-7) ë°±ì—… í•˜ì§€ ì•Šê³  = 'y' Enter ('y' = NO BACKUP):
__EOF__
        read restore_only ; echo "${uuu}"
        if [ "x$restore_only" = "xy" ]; then
            N_is_current_no_backup="n"
        else
            N_is_current_no_backup="y"
        fi
        echo "[ í˜„ì¬ DB ë¥¼ ë°±ì—…í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ = ${restore_only} ]"

        #-- ----> í˜„ì¬ì˜ DB ë¥¼ ë°±ì—…í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ”ë‹¤ ì„ íƒ.
    fi

    echo "qq2----> N_is_current_no_backup = [ ${N_is_current_no_backup} ]"
    if [ "x$N_is_current_no_backup" != 'xn' ]; then
        echo "x$N_is_current_no_backup != 'xn'"
    else
        echo "x$N_is_current_no_backup = 'xn'"
    fi
    echo "qq2----> restore_only = [ ${restore_only} ]"

    if [ "x$N_is_current_no_backup" != 'xn' ]; then
        #-- ----> í˜„ì¬ DB ë¥¼ ë‹¤ìš´ë¡œë“œ + ë°±ì—… í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

        current_backup_7z="${LOCAL_Y2M2}/last-${DATABASE_CONTAINER}-$(date +%y%m%d_%H%M%S)-$(uname -n).sql.7z"
        cat <<__EOF__
(6-8) ì§€ì •í•œ ë°±ì—…íŒŒì¼ì„ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ì— ë¶“ê¸° ì „ì—,
      í˜„ì¬ ìš´ì˜ì¤‘ì¸ DB ë¥¼ ë¨¼ì € ${LOCAL_Y2M2} ì— ë°±ì—…í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

      time sudo docker exec ${DATABASE_CONTAINER} pg_dumpall -U ${DB_user_NAME} | 7za a -mx=9 -p -si ${current_backup_7z}

ğŸ–ï¸ (6-9) ë°±ì—…í•˜ëŠ” .7z íŒŒì¼ì— ì§€ì •í•´ ì¤„ ìƒˆë¡œìš´ ===ë¹„ë°€ë²ˆí˜¸=== ë¥¼ ì…ë ¥í•˜ì„¸ìš”.

__EOF__
        time sudo docker exec ${DATABASE_CONTAINER} pg_dumpall -U ${DB_user_NAME} | 7za a -mx=9 -p -si ${current_backup_7z}
        cat <<__EOF__
(6-10) ì˜¤ëŠ˜ ìš”ì¼ì´ë¦„ì˜ íŒŒì¼ì„ í´ë¼ìš°ë“œë¡œ ë³µì‚¬í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
      time rclone copy ${current_backup_7z} ${CLOUD_NAME}:${CLOUD_Y2M2}/
__EOF__
        time rclone copy ${current_backup_7z} ${CLOUD_NAME}:${CLOUD_Y2M2}/
        cat <<__EOF__
(6-11) í´ë¼ìš°ë“œ í´ë”ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.
       time rclone lsl ${CLOUD_NAME}:${CLOUD_Y2M2}
__EOF__
        time rclone lsl ${CLOUD_NAME}:${CLOUD_Y2M2}

        #-- <---- í˜„ì¬ DB ë¥¼ ë‹¤ìš´ë¡œë“œ + ë°±ì—… í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
    fi

    cat <<__EOF__
(6-12) ê¸°ì¡´ì˜ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ë¥¼ ì‚­ì œí•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
       time sudo docker exec -it ${DATABASE_CONTAINER} dropdb -U ${DB_user_NAME} ${DATABASE_NAME}
__EOF__
    time sudo docker exec -it ${DATABASE_CONTAINER} dropdb -U ${DB_user_NAME} ${DATABASE_NAME}
cat <<__EOF__
(6-13) ë¹ˆ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ë¥¼ ìƒˆë¡œ ë§Œë“­ë‹ˆë‹¤.
       time sudo docker exec -it ${DATABASE_CONTAINER} createdb -U ${DB_user_NAME} ${DATABASE_NAME}
__EOF__

    cat <<__EOF__
(6-14) ì§€ì •í•œ ë°±ì—…íŒŒì¼ì„ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ì— ë‹¤ì‹œ ë¶“ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. (RESTORE)

       time 7za x -so ${zzz} | sudo docker exec -i ${DATABASE_CONTAINER} psql -U ${DB_user_NAME} ${DATABASE_NAME}

ğŸ–ï¸ (6-15) ë°±ì—…í• ë•Œ ì…ë ¥í•œ ----ë¹„ë°€ë²ˆí˜¸---- ë¥¼ ì…ë ¥í•˜ì„¸ìš”.

__EOF__
    time 7za x -so ${zzz} | sudo docker exec -i ${DATABASE_CONTAINER} psql -U ${DB_user_NAME} ${DATABASE_NAME}
    cat <<__EOF__
(6-16) ë©ˆì·„ë˜ ìœ„í‚¤ ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆë¥¼ ë‹¤ì‹œ ì‹œì‘í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
       sudo docker start ${WIKI_CONTAINER} ; sudo docker ps -a
__EOF__
    sudo docker start ${WIKI_CONTAINER} ; sudo docker ps -a
    echo "(6-17) ë°±ì—… ì‘ì—…ì´ ëë‚¬ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤."
    #-- <---- ë¦¬ìŠ¤í† ì–´ í•  .7z íŒŒì¼ì´ ìˆë‹¤.
fi
zzz=""
echo "ğŸ¶ (6-18) --------------------"
```

3. orangepi zero 2w ì˜ ubuntu ì—ì„œ ~/.bashrc ì— ì¶”ê°€í•˜ëŠ” ë¶€ë¶„.
```
# ~/.bashrc: executed by bash(1) for non-login shells.
# see /usr/share/doc/bash/examples/startup-files (in the package bash-doc)
# for examples

# If not running interactively, don't do anything
case $- in
    *i*) ;;
      *) return;;
esac

# don't put duplicate lines or lines starting with space in the history.
# See bash(1) for more options
HISTCONTROL=ignoreboth

# append to the history file, don't overwrite it
shopt -s histappend

# for setting history length see HISTSIZE and HISTFILESIZE in bash(1)
HISTSIZE=1000
HISTFILESIZE=2000

# check the window size after each command and, if necessary,
# update the values of LINES and COLUMNS.
shopt -s checkwinsize

# If set, the pattern "**" used in a pathname expansion context will
# match all files and zero or more directories and subdirectories.
#shopt -s globstar

# make less more friendly for non-text input files, see lesspipe(1)
[ -x /usr/bin/lesspipe ] && eval "$(SHELL=/bin/sh lesspipe)"

# set variable identifying the chroot you work in (used in the prompt below)
if [ -z "${debian_chroot:-}" ] && [ -r /etc/debian_chroot ]; then
    debian_chroot=$(cat /etc/debian_chroot)
fi

# set a fancy prompt (non-color, unless we know we "want" color)
case "$TERM" in
    xterm-color|*-256color) color_prompt=yes;;
esac

# uncomment for a colored prompt, if the terminal has the capability; turned
# off by default to not distract the user: the focus in a terminal window
# should be on the output of commands, not on the prompt
#force_color_prompt=yes

if [ -n "$force_color_prompt" ]; then
    if [ -x /usr/bin/tput ] && tput setaf 1 >&/dev/null; then
        # We have color support; assume it's compliant with Ecma-48
        # (ISO/IEC-6429). (Lack of such support is extremely rare, and such
        # a case would tend to support setf rather than setaf.)
        color_prompt=yes
    else
        color_prompt=
    fi
fi

if [ "$color_prompt" = yes ]; then
    PS1='${debian_chroot:+($debian_chroot)}\[\033[01;32m\]\u@\h\[\033[00m\]:\[\033[01;34m\]\w\[\033[00m\]\$ '
else
    PS1='${debian_chroot:+($debian_chroot)}\u@\h:\w\$ '
fi
unset color_prompt force_color_prompt

# If this is an xterm set the title to user@host:dir
case "$TERM" in
xterm*|rxvt*)
    PS1="\[\e]0;${debian_chroot:+($debian_chroot)}\u@\h: \w\a\]$PS1"
    ;;
*)
    ;;
esac

# enable color support of ls and also add handy aliases
if [ -x /usr/bin/dircolors ]; then
    test -r ~/.dircolors && eval "$(dircolors -b ~/.dircolors)" || eval "$(dircolors -b)"
    alias ls='ls --color=auto'
    #alias dir='dir --color=auto'
    #alias vdir='vdir --color=auto'

    alias grep='grep --color=auto'
    alias fgrep='fgrep --color=auto'
    alias egrep='egrep --color=auto'
fi

# colored GCC warnings and errors
#export GCC_COLORS='error=01;31:warning=01;35:note=01;36:caret=01;32:locus=01:quote=01'

# some more ls aliases
alias ll='ls -alF'
alias la='ls -A'
alias l='ls -CF'

# Add an "alert" alias for long running commands.  Use like so:
#   sleep 10; alert
alias alert='notify-send --urgency=low -i "$([ $? = 0 ] && echo terminal || echo error)" "$(history|tail -n1|sed -e '\''s/^\s*[0-9]\+\s*//;s/[;&|]\s*alert$//'\'')"'

# Alias definitions.
# You may want to put all your additions into a separate file like
# ~/.bash_aliases, instead of adding them here directly.
# See /usr/share/doc/bash-doc/examples in the bash-doc package.

if [ -f ~/.bash_aliases ]; then
    . ~/.bash_aliases
fi

# enable programmable completion features (you don't need to enable
# this, if it's already enabled in /etc/bash.bashrc and /etc/profile
# sources /etc/bash.bashrc).
if ! shopt -oq posix; then
  if [ -f /usr/share/bash-completion/bash_completion ]; then
    . /usr/share/bash-completion/bash_completion
  elif [ -f /etc/bash_completion ]; then
    . /etc/bash_completion
  fi
fi

#----> ë¶€í„° ì¶”ê°€
# ..... user 3x:ê¸€ììƒ‰ 4x:ë°”íƒ•ìƒ‰ 0íšŒ 1ë¹¨ 2ì´ˆ 3ë…¸ 4ì²­ 5ë³´ 6íŒŒ 7í°
# 00 01 02 íë¦¼ 03 ì´íƒ¤ë¦­ 04 ë°‘ì¤„ 05 ê¹œë¹¡ê±°ë¦¼ 06 07 ë°˜ì „ 08 09 ê¸€ìì— ì¤„ê¸‹ê¸° 10
PS1='\e[0;36m\t\e[0m\e[0;33m\D{%a}\e[0;35m\D{%y}\e[0;36m\D{%m}\e[0;31m\D{%d} \e[0;36m\u\e[0;33m@\e[0;34m\h\e[0m \e[04;32m\w\e[0m\n\W $ '
#........ 11:35:04 .......... í™” .......... 23 .......... 10 .......... 17 ........ yosj ..... @ . orangepizero2w .. ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ì „ì²´ .. ì¤„ë°”ê¾¸ê³  ìµœì¢…ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬
export EDITOR=vi
alias rm='rm -i'
alias cp='cp -i'
alias mv='mv -i'
alias more='more -e'
alias ls='ls --color=auto'
alias ll='ls -l --color=auto'
alias grep='grep --color=auto'
#<---- ê¹Œì§€ ì¶”ê°€
```
